 This section, sometimes considered a dedicated voter of the Congress, sometimes bets on the Samajwadi Party or the Bahujan Samaj Party for the last two decades and also speaks of the same party in state power
 ab jabaki chunaav kii tarikhon kaa elaan ho chukaa he tab sabaki nigahen isi baat par hai ki muslim voton par kis party kaa bharosa khara utrega or kise maayusi haath lagegi
 Every fifth voter of the state is Muslim
 If you consider the 2011 census as the basis, then there are about 19 in UP
 26 fisadi aabaadi yani 3
 84 crore people are Muslims
 mana jaataa he ki upi kii kareeb 150 siten aisi hai jahaan muslim vot 20 se 30 fisadi ke aasapaas he
 They play a key role in the defeat and victory of the candidates
 2012 ke vidhansabha chunaav main pehali baar upi main sarvaadhik 64 musalmaan vidhayak bane
 When every fifth voter of the state comes from this section, it is the compulsion of every party who is involved in the fight for power in the state to lure or strategize by keeping it at the center
 sapa, basapa or congress jahaan is varg ko lubhaane kii har mumkin koshish karti hai to bijepi jaanati he ki muslim uske swaabhaavik voter nahin hai isliye uski ranneeti is tabake ke voton main vibhaajan kii rahati he
 When the Bahujan Samaj Party in 2007 and the Samajwadi Party won the historic mandate in 2012, the biggest reason for their victory was their outright Muslim votes with the Dalit and OBC respectively
 maaya kii list main haaavee rahe jaateey samikarndo din pehle jab basapa supremeo mayawati ne apane tikaton kii suchi kaa jaateey ganit samajhaayaa to bataaya ki kul 403 siton main se essi ke 87, muslim 97, obisi 106 or agadi jati ke 113 ummidavaar hai
 That is why BSP leaders raise issues like Muzaffarnagar, Dadri in every attack on the state government
 bijepi netaa dayashankar singh kii mayawati par abhadra tippanee ke prakaran main nasimuddin siddiki ke peeche party isiilie majbootee se khadi rahi kyonki unhen basapa kaa sabase bada muslim cheharaa mana jaataa he
 On the other hand, in the Samajwadi Party, Azam Khan's tutti speaks because it is his responsibility to get Muslim votes to SP

 Prime Minister Narendra Modi has summoned Biplab Deb for his controversial statements
 party sutron ke mutabikbiplab debko dilli aane ke liye kaha gaya he
 Deb has been asked to meet PM Modi and BJP President Amit Shah on May 2 in the national capital
 sutron ke mutabik party ke varisht netaa deb ke bayanon se paidaa hue vivaad se naaraaz hai
 Deb is going to speak anything, Modi will talk to him
 bataa den ki deb ko tripura ke mukhyamantri pad kii shapath liye abhi do maheene bhi nahin hua or unhone kai aise bayaan die hai, jinaki vyapak aalochana hui he
 Recently he was in the discussion by giving peculiar advice to the students preparing for civil service
 deb ne kaha ki sirf civil ejiniers ko hi civil sarvice pariksha ke liye aavedan karnaa chahie
 His reasoning behind this is also surprising
 unka kahana he ki maikenical ejineering karne ke baad civil services main nahin janaa chahie
 This statement of Biplab Deb came after the result of the civil service examination
 isse pehle biplab deb mahabharat kaal main internet or miss world main indian beauty ko lekar bhivivaadit bayaande chuke hai
 Giving a new scientific theory, he claimed that the Internet was also in the era of Mahabharata and was used then
 unhone yah bhi daawa kiya tha ki us yug main satellite bhi maujuud the
 Biplab Kumar Debne has also questioned the title of Miss World in 1997 to Diana Hayden
 unhone kaha tha ki dyna heden kii jeet fiks thi
 While praising Aishwarya Rai, she said that Aishwarya represents Indian women in the true sense
 desh main samay samay par hone vaali dharmaataran kii ghatnaon par roak lagane ke liye kanoon banane kaa kendra sarkaar ke paas koi prastaav nahin he
 In a written reply to Prahlad Joshi's question in the Lok Sabha today, Minister of State for Home Ajay Maken said that reports related to his alleged involvement in the conversion of some places are received from time to time
 unhone kaha ki bharat ke samvidhan ke anusaar lok vyavastha or police rajya ke vishay hai atah aparaadhon kii rokthaam pataa lagaana or panjikaran karnaa jaanch karnaa mukhyatah rajya sarkaron or sangh shasit prashasano kaa vishay he
 He said that there is no proposal to enact a law to stop conversion
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh or unke pakistani samakaksh navaj sharif ke bich neuyork main is maheene ke aakhir main vaarta ke asaar najar aane ke bich bharat ne kaha he ki baithak ke liye ek sauhardpurn maahaul jaruri he
 Pakistan has informed India that it has named a new prosecutor for the long-pending Mumbai attack hearing and will send a judicial commission there on 23 September to cross-examine key Indian witnesses, making concrete progress in the investigation
 The demand for New Delhi will be met to some extent
 videshmantri salmaan khurshid ne kaha ki pakistani pradhanmantri ke videsh maamalon ke salaahkaar sartaaj ajij ne unhen guuruuvaar kii raat kirgistan kii rajdhani main ek anaupchaarik baatcheet ke dauraan is ghatnakram kii jaankaree di
 Aziz said he had a good meeting with Khurshid and that diplomatic efforts would continue in New York later this month to encourage dialogue between the Prime Ministers of the two countries beyond the UN General Assembly
 khurshid or ajij shanghai sahyog sanghathan (essio) sammelan main shaamil hone ke liye yahaan aae hue hai
 Khurshid, who attended the dinner with Aziz, said, "we hope and hope that prosecutors will be appointed soon
" nyaayik ayog dwaara ekatra kiye jane vaale saboot pakistani adaalat ko uplabdh karaae jaaenge
 The former prosecutor was murdered
 unhone bataaya ki ajij ne unase kaha ki nyaayik ayog 23 sitambar ko bharat kii yatra par jayega
 The comments unhone samvaadadaataaon se kaha, ham iskaa swaagat karte hai or ham abhiyojak kii niyukti kaa swaagat karte hai
 Khurshid said, and we truly, sincerely hope that things will move fast now and we will see through the court proceedings that some concrete things are happening
 videshmantri ne bataaya ki unhone ajij ko is baat se avgat karaayaa ki donon deshon ke pradhanmantriyon ke bich sambhavit baithak ke liye ek sauhardpurn maahaul kii jarurat hogi
 He said that Prime Minister Manmohan Singh has also repeatedly expressed this stance
 khurshid ne kaha, hamane ajij se kaha ki sakaaratmak vaarta kii logon kii ichha ke maddenjar ek sauhardpurn maahaul hona chahie
 Whenever there is a high level of dialogue, the atmosphere is good
 unhone bharat-paak seemaa par shanti kii jarurat par jor dete hue kaha ki niyantran rekha par sangharsh viraam kaa sammaan avashya kiya janaa chahie

 Uttarakhand Chief Minister Trivendra Singh Rawat has urged people not to use polythene

 Plastic bags have been banned at all places in Uttarakhand

 engiti or ucch nyaayalay ke sakht adeshon ke baad ab soobe kii trivendra sarkaar ne bhi uttarakhand ko polithin mukt rajya banane kaa sankalp le liya he
 From now on, if any person or businessman is found to be using polythene, he will be fined heavily
 polithin kaa istemaal karne par dukandaaron par 5000 rupee, theli waalon par 2000 rupee, graahakon par 500 rupee tak kaa jurmaana lagegaa
 The CM appealed to the people of the state to stop using polythene keeping in mind the environment and give their support in this campaign
 polithin ke saath hi thermokol or plastic se bane plate or glass kii bikri par rajdhani kshetra main purna pratiband laga diya gaya he
 At the same time, a campaign is being organized by teams formed by the municipal administration to ban the sale of plate and glass made of polyethylene and thermocol

 Shopkeepers will be charged a fine of up to Rs 5000
 vahiin kisi vyakti vishesh se 500 rupye kaa jurmaana vasula jayega
